  <script>
   var Avianca = Avianca || {};
    
    Avianca.Mobile = function(){
    	/**
         * Get query parameters
         */
        this.getQueryVariable = function(variable){
            var query = window.location.search.substring(1);
            var vars = query.split("&");
            for (var i=0;i<vars.length;i++) {
                    var pair = vars[i].split("=");
                    if(pair[0] == variable){
                    	return pair[1];
                    }
            }
            return(false);
        }
        
        /**
         * Whether a cookie to override mobile versions exists or not.
         */
        this.checkMobileCookie = function(){
        	return (document.cookie.replace(/(?:(?:^|.*;\s*)reqfromappmobile\s*\=\s*([^;]*).*$)|^.*$/, "$1") === "true");
        }
    }
    
    var aviancaMobile = new Avianca.Mobile();
            
    // Render desktop site if there is a cookie or whether the URL comes with specified parameter
    if(aviancaMobile.checkMobileCookie() || aviancaMobile.getQueryVariable("reqfromappmobile") === "true"){    	
    	if(!aviancaMobile.checkMobileCookie()){    	    
    		document.cookie = "reqfromappmobile=true";
    	}
    }else{
    	if(WURFL.is_mobile === true && WURFL.form_factor !== "Tablet"){				
    		var mobileUrl = "";
        	
    		window.location = mobileUrl !== "" ? mobileUrl : "http://m.avianca.com/";
    	}
    }
  </script>

  dataLayerObjName = 'gtmDt';

  domain = 'avianca.com';
  domainRegExp = new RegExp(/((avianca|e\-travel|amadeus)\.com)|amadeus\.net$/gi);

  function getFullMonth(month) {
    switch (month.toString()) {
      case '01':
      case '1':
        var ptMonth = 'January';
        break;
      case '02':
      case '2':
        var ptMonth = 'February';
        break;
      case '03':
      case '3':
        var ptMonth = 'March';
        break;
      case '04':
      case '4':
        var ptMonth = 'April';
        break;
      case '05':
      case '5':
        var ptMonth = 'May';
        break;
      case '06':
      case '6':
        var ptMonth = 'June';
        break;
      case '07':
      case '7':
        var ptMonth = 'July';
        break;
      case '08':
      case '8':
        var ptMonth = 'August';
        break;
      case '09':
      case '9':
        var ptMonth = 'September';
        break;
      case '10':
        var ptMonth = 'October';
        break;
      case '11':
        var ptMonth = 'November';
        break;
      case '12':
        var ptMonth = 'December';
        break;
      default:
        return month;
    }

    return ptMonth;
  }

  function getWeekDay(weekday) {
    switch (weekday.toString()) {
      case '0':
        var ptMonth = 'Sunday';
        break;
      case '1':
        var ptMonth = 'Monday';
        break;
      case '2':
        var ptMonth = 'Tuesday';
        break;
      case '3':
        var ptMonth = 'Wednesday';
        break;
      case '4':
        var ptMonth = 'Thursday';
        break;
      case '5':
        var ptMonth = 'Friday';
        break;
      case '6':
        var ptMonth = 'Saturday';
        break;
      case '7':
        var ptMonth = 'Sunday';
        break;
      default:
        return weekday;
    }

    return ptMonth;
  }

  function getCookie(check_name) {
    //first we'll split this cookie up into name/value pairs
    //note: document.cookie only returns name=value, not the other components
    var a_all_cookies = document.cookie.split(';');
    var a_temp_cookie = '';
    var cookie_name = '';
    var cookie_value = '';
    var b_cookie_found = false; // set boolean t/f default f

    for (i = 0; i < a_all_cookies.length; i++) {
      // now we'll split apart each name=value pair
      a_temp_cookie = a_all_cookies[i].split('=');
      // and trim left/right whitespace while we're at it
      cookie_name = a_temp_cookie[0].replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, '');
      // if the extracted name matches passed check_name
      if (cookie_name == check_name) {
        b_cookie_found = true;
        // we need to handle case where cookie has no value but exists (no = sign, that is):
        if (a_temp_cookie.length > 1) {
          cookie_value = unescape(a_temp_cookie.slice(1).join('=').replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, ''));
        }
        // note that in cases where cookie is initialized but no value, null is returned
        return cookie_value;
        break;
      }
      a_temp_cookie = null;
      cookie_name = '';
    }
    if (!b_cookie_found) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  function setCookie(cname, cvalue, exdays) {
    var expires = "";
    if (exdays != null) {
      var d = new Date();
      d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
      expires = ";expires=" + d.toUTCString();
    }
    document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + expires + ";domain=." + domain + ";path=/";
  }

      })();
      obj.recognized = (function(){ try{ var cookieValue = getCookie('recognized'); return (cookieValue != null);}catch(e){return false;}; })(); // If the user has ever logged to the website (Boolean)
      obj.lastVisitDays = (function(){ try{ return (lastVisit != null ? Math.floor((today-parseInt(lastVisit))/86400000) : null);}catch(e){return null;}; })(); // Days since last visit (Interger)
      obj.lastSearchDays = (function(){ try{ return (lastSearch != null ? Math.floor((today-parseInt(lastSearch.timestamp))/86400000) : null);}catch(e){return null;}; })(); // Days since last visit (Integer)

      obj.lastBoughtRoute = (function(){ try{ return (lastTransaction != null ? lastTransaction.Trayecto : null);}catch(e){return null;}; })(); // Last Purchased Route (String)
      obj.userInfo = (function(){ try{ if (document.cookie.indexOf('AVSESSION_ID') == -1) { setCookie('userInfo','',0); return null; }; var cookieValue = getCookie('userInfo'); return JSON.parse(cookieValue);}catch(e){return null;}; })(); // User Info JSON String '{name:(String),lastName:(String),lifeMiles:(String),sessionToken:(String),message:(String)}'
      return obj;
    })(),
    page: {
      owner: 'Avianca', // Fixed value (String)

            path: (function(currentPageName){ // Bahavior Path (Concatenated Page Name) **Cookie must be Session based** (String)
                try{

    visit: (function() {
      var obj = {},
        today = new Date();
        obj.holiday = (function(){ try{ var cookieValue = getCookie('holiday'); return JSON.parse(cookieValue) || {loaded:false};}catch(e){return {loaded:false};}; })(); // JSON String containing holiday information '{loaded:(Boolean),publicHoliday:(Boolean),holidayType:(String),holidayRegion:(String)}' **The cookie should be session based**
        obj.location = (function(){ try{ var cookieValue = getCookie('location'); return JSON.parse(cookieValue) || {loaded:false};}catch(e){return {loaded:false};}; })(); // JSON String containing location '{loaded:(Boolean),region:(String),city:(String),zip:(String)}' **The cookie should be session based**
        obj.weather = (function(){ try{ var cookieValue = getCookie('weather'); return JSON.parse(cookieValue) || {loaded:false};}catch(e){return {loaded:false};}; })(); // JSON String containing weather '{loaded:(Boolean),temp:(Integer),weather:(String)}' **The cookie should be session based**
      try {
